If not done no new events will be emitted for this key.\\n46: // If an event handling is marked as failed the configured error handler is called\\n47: // (WithErrorHandler). The default error handler will requeue the event (by its key) for\\n48: // later retried processing. The requeueing is rate limited and can be configured with\\n49: // WithRateLimiter option to Events().\\n50: //\\n51: // The resource is lazy, e.g. it will not start the informer until a call\\n52: // has been made to Events() or Store().\\n53: type Resource[T k8sRuntime.Object] interface {\\n54: \\t// Resource can be observed either via Observe() or via Events(). The observable\\n55: \\t// is implemented in terms of Events() and same semantics apply.\\n56: \\tstream.Observable[Event[T]]\\n57: \\n58: \\t// Events returns a channel of events. Each event must be marked as handled\\n59: \\t// with a call to Done() which marks the key processed. No new events for this key\\n60: \\t// will be emitted before Done() is called.\\n61: \\t//\\n62: \\t// A missing Done() will lead to an eventual panic (via finalizer on Event[T]).\\n63: \\t// Panic on this situation is needed as otherwise no new events would be emitted\\n64: \\t// and thus this needs to be enforced.\\n65: \\t//\\n66: \\t// A stream of Upsert events are emitted first to replay the current state of the\\n67: \\t// store after which incremental upserts and deletes follow until the underlying\\n68: \\t// store is synchronized after which a Sync event is emitted and further incremental\\n69: \\t// updates:\\n70: \\t//\\n71: \\t//\\t(start observing), Upsert, Upsert, Upsert, (done replaying store contents), Upsert, Upsert,\\n72: \\t//\\t  (store synchronized with API server), Sync, Upsert, Delete, Upsert, ...\\n73: \\t//\\n74: \\t// The emitting of the Sync event does not depend on whether or not Upsert events have\\n75: \\t// all been marked Done() without an error. The sync event solely signals that the underlying\\n76: \\t// store has synchronized and that Upsert events for objects in a synchronized store have been\\n77: \\t// sent to the observer.\\n78: \\t//\\n79: \\t// When Done() is called with non-nil error the error handler is invoked, which\\n80: \\t// can ignore, requeue the event (by key) or close the channel. The default error handler\\n81: \\t// will requeue.\\n82: \\t//\\n83: \\t// If an Upsert is retried and the object has been deleted, a Delete event will be emitted instead.\\n84: \\t// Conversely if a Delete event is retried and the object has been recreated with the same key,\\n85: \\t// an Upsert will be emitted instead.\\n86: \\t//\\n87: \\t// If an objects is created and immediately deleted, then a slow observer may not observe this at\\n88: \\t// all. In all cases a Delete event is only emitted if the observer has seen an Upsert. Whether or\\n89: \\t// not it had been successfully handled (via Done(nil)) does not affect this property.\\n90: \\tEvents(ctx context.Context, opts ...EventsOpt) <-chan Event[T]\\n91: \\n92: \\t// Store retrieves the read-only store for the resource. Blocks until\\n93: \\t// the store has been synchronized or the context cancelled.\\n94: \\t// Returns a non-nil error if context is cancelled or the resource\\n95: \\t// has been stopped before store has synchronized.\\n96: \\tStore(context.Context) (Store[T], error)\\n97: }\\n98: \\n99: // New creates a new Resource[T]. access to a Kubernetes resource through either\\n34: // a stream of events or a read-only store.\\n35: //\\n36: // Observing of the events can be done from a constructor as subscriber\\n37: // registration is non-blocking.\\n38: //\\n39: // Store() however should only be called from a start hook, or from a\\n40: // goroutine forked from the start hook as it blocks until the store\\n41: // has been synchronized.\\n42: //\\n43: // The subscriber can process the events from Events() asynchronously and in\\n44: // parallel, but for each event the Done() function must be called to mark\\n45: // the event as handled. If not done no new events will be emitted for this key.\\n46: // If an event handling is marked as failed the configured error handler is called\\n47: // (WithErrorHandler). The default error handler will requeue the event (by its key) for\\n48: // later retried processing. The requeueing is rate limited and can be configured with\\n49: // WithRateLimiter option to Events().\\n50: //\\n51: // The resource is lazy, e.g. it will not start the informer until a call\\n52: // has been made to Events() or Store().\\n53: type Resource[T k8sRuntime.Object] interface {\\n54: \\t// Resource can be observed either via Observe() or via Events(). The observable\\n55: \\t// is implemented in terms of Events() and same semantics apply.\\n56: \\tstream.Observable[Event[T]]\\n57: \\n58: \\t// Events returns a channel of events. Each event must be marked as handled\\n59: \\t// with a call to Done() which marks the key processed. No new events for this key\\n60: \\t// will be emitted before Done() is called.\\n61: \\t//\\n62: \\t// A missing Done() will lead to an eventual panic (via finalizer on Event[T]).\\n63: \\t// Panic on this situation is needed as otherwise no new events would be emitted\\n64: \\t// and thus this needs to be enforced.\\n65: \\t//\\n66: \\t// A stream of Upsert events are emitted first to replay the current state of the\\n67: \\t// store after which incremental upserts and deletes follow until the underlying\\n68: \\t// store is synchronized after which a Sync event is emitted and further incremental\\n69: \\t// updates:\\n70: \\t//\\n71: \\t//\\t(start observing), Upsert, Upsert, Upsert, (done replaying store contents), Upsert, Upsert,\\n72: \\t//\\t  (store synchronized with API server), Sync, Upsert, Delete, Upsert, ...\\n73: \\t//\\n74: \\t// The emitting of the Sync event does not depend on whether or not Upsert events have\\n75: \\t// all been marked Done() without an error. The sync event solely signals that the underlying\\n76: \\t// store has synchronized and that Upsert events for objects in a synchronized store have been\\n77: \\t// sent to the observer.\\n78: \\t//\\n79: \\t// When Done() is called with non-nil error the error handler is invoked, which\\n80: \\t// can ignore, requeue the event (by key) or close the channel. The default error handler\\n81: \\t// will requeue.\\n82: \\t//\\n83: \\t// If an Upsert is retried and the object has been deleted, a Delete event will be emitted instead.\\n84: \\t// Conversely if a Delete event is retried and the object has been recreated with the same key,\\n85: \\t// an Upsert will be emitted instead.\\n86: \\t//\\n87: \\t// If an objects is created and immediately deleted, then a slow observer may not observe this at\\n88: \\t// all. In all cases a Delete event is only emitted if the observer has seen an Upsert. Whether or\\n89: \\t// not it had been successfully handled (via Done(nil)) does not affect this property.\\n90: \\tEvents(ctx context.Context, opts ...EventsOpt) <-chan Event[T]\\n91: \\n92: \\t// Store retrieves the read-only store for the resource. Blocks until\\n93: \\t// the store has been synchronized or the context cancelled.\\n94: \\t// Returns a non-nil error if context is cancelled or the resource\\n95: \\t// has been stopped before store has synchronized.\\n96: \\tStore(context.Context) (Store[T], error)\\n97: }\\n98: \\n99: // New creates a new Resource[T]. A value of 0 means unlimited.\nfunc NewPolicyQuotaController(\n\tmaxPerNamespace int,\n\tciliumNetworkPolicies resource.Resource[*cilium_v2.CiliumNetworkPolicy],\n) *PolicyQuotaController {\n\treturn &PolicyQuotaController{\n\t\tlog:                   log,\n\t\tnamespacePolicyCounts: make(map[string]int),\n\t\tmaxPerNamespace:       maxPerNamespace,\n\t\tciliumNetworkPolicies: ciliumNetworkPolicies,\n\t}\n}\n\n// CheckQuota checks if a new policy can be created in the given namespace.\n// Returns an error if the quota would be exceeded.\nfunc (p *PolicyQuotaController) CheckQuota(namespace string) error {\n\tif p.maxPerNamespace == 0 {\n\t\t// Unlimited quota\n\t\treturn nil\n\t}\n\n\tp.mu.RLock()\n\tdefer p.mu.RUnlock()\n\n\tcount := p.namespacePolicyCounts[namespace]\n\tif count >= p.maxPerNamespace {\n\t\treturn fmt.Errorf(\n\t\t\t\"policy quota exceeded for namespace %q: %d/%d policies\",\n\t\t\tnamespace, count, PolicyQuotaController Implementation Summary\n\n## Overview\nThis implementation adds a `PolicyQuotaController` to Cilium that enforces per-namespace limits on the number of `CiliumNetworkPolicy` resources, preventing policy sprawl in multi-tenant clusters.\n\n## Files Created\n\n### 1. `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/types_policy_quota.go`\nDefines the Kubernetes CRD types for `CiliumPolicyQuota`:\n\n- **CiliumPolicyQuota**: Main CRD struct\n  - TypeMeta and ObjectMeta (standard Kubernetes fields)\n  - Spec: CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec (desired state)\n  - Status: CiliumPolicyQuotaStatus (current state)\n\n- **CiliumPolicyQuotaSpec**: Configuration spec\n  - MaxPoliciesPerNamespace: Maximum policies allowed per namespace (0 = unlimited)\n\n- **CiliumPolicyQuotaStatus**: Current status tracking\n  - NamespaceStatus: Map of namespace to NamespacePolicyStatus\n\n- **NamespacePolicyStatus**: Per-namespace status info\n  - CurrentCount: Number of policies in namespace\n  - MaxCount: Maximum allowed in namespace\n  - LastUpdated: Last update timestamp\n\n- **CiliumPolicyQuotaList**: List wrapper for CiliumPolicyQuota resources\n\n**Key Features:**\n- Cluster-scoped resource (not namespaced)\n- Full Kubernetes code generation support (genclient, deepcopy-gen, etc.)\n- Kubebuilder annotations for CRD generation\n- Follows Cilium CRD patterns\n\n### 2. `pkg/policy/quota/controller.go`\nMain controller implementation:\n\n- **PolicyQuotaController**: Core controller struct\n  - Thread-safe namespace policy counting using sync.RWMutex\n  - Watches CiliumNetworkPolicy resources\n  - Enforces per-namespace quotas\n\n- **Key Methods:**\n  - `NewPolicyQuotaController()`: Constructor\n  - `Run(ctx context.Context) error`: Main controller loop\n  - `CheckQuota(namespace string) error`: Enforces quota checks\n  - `GetNamespacePolicyCount(namespace string) int`: Retrieves current count\n  - `handleEvent()`: Processes resource events (Upsert, Delete, Sync)\n\n**Functionality:**\n- Watches CiliumNetworkPolicy resources via `resource.Resource[T]`\n- Increments count on Upsert events\n- Decrements count on Delete events\n- Logs operations using Cilium's standard logging framework\n- Thread-safe concurrent access to policy counts\n- Support for unlimited quotas (maxPerNamespace = 0)\n\n### 3. `pkg/k8s/apis/cilium.io/v2/register.go`\nKubernetes scheme registration:\n\n- Added CiliumPolicyQuota and CiliumPolicyQuotaList constants\n- Updated `addKnownTypes()` function to register the new types\n- Follows existing Cilium registration patterns\n\n**Constants Added:**\n- `CPQPluralName = \"ciliumpolicyquotas\"`\n- `CPQKindDefinition = \"CiliumPolicyQuota\"`\n- `CPQName = \"ciliumpolicyquotas.cilium.io\"`\n\n### 4. `pkg/policy/quota/controller_test.go`\nComprehensive test suite:\n\n**Mock Implementation:**\n- `mockResource`: Full mock of `resource.Resource[T]` interface\n- Implements Events(), Observe(), and Store() methods\n- Allows async event injection for testing\n\n**Test Coverage:**\n1. `TestNewPolicyQuotaController`: Constructor validation\n2. `TestCheckQuotaUnlimited`: Unlimited quota behavior\n3. `TestCheckQuotaExceeded`: Quota enforcement\n4. `TestCheckQuotaWithinLimit`: Valid quota scenarios\n5. `TestHandleEventUpsert`: Policy creation tracking\n6. `TestHandleEventDelete`: Policy deletion tracking\n7. `TestHandleEventSync`: Sync event handling\n8. `TestMultipleNamespaces`: Multi-namespace isolation\n9. `TestRunContextCancellation`: Context cancellation handling\n10. `TestRunEventProcessing`: Controller main loop\n11. `TestGetNamespacePolicyCount`: Count retrieval\n12. `TestThreadSafety`: Concurrent access validation\n\n## Design Patterns Used\n\n### Cilium Patterns:\n- **Resource Watching**: Uses `resource.Resource[T]` from Cilium's k8s package\n- **Event-Driven**: Processes Upsert, Delete, and Sync events\n- **Logging**: Uses Cilium's structured logging with logfields\n- **Thread Safety**: RWMutex for concurrent access\n\n### Kubernetes Patterns:\n- **CRD Structure**: Standard TypeMeta, ObjectMeta, Spec, Status layout\n- **Code Generation**: Uses Kubernetes code-gen annotations\n- **Scheme Registration**: Proper registration for client-go compatibility\n\n### Go Patterns:\n- **Constructor Pattern**: NewPolicyQuotaController for object creation\n- **Defer Cleanup**: defer/unlock pattern for mutex safety\n- **Interface Implementation**: Full interface satisfaction for resource.Resource\n\n## Usage Example\n\n```go\n// Create controller\ncontroller := NewPolicyQuotaController(\n    maxPerNamespace, // 0 for unlimited\n    ciliumNetworkPolicies, // resource.Resource[*CiliumNetworkPolicy]\n)\n\n// Check quota before allowing policy creation\nif err := controller.CheckQuota(\"default\"); err != nil {\n    // Quota exceeded, reject policy\n    return err\n}\n\n// Start controller to watch policies\ngo controller.Run(ctx)\n\n// Later: get current count\ncount := controller.GetNamespacePolicyCount(\"default\")\n```\n\n## Key Implementation Details\n\n1. **Thread Safety**: Uses `sync.RWMutex` to protect the `namespacePolicyCounts` map\n2. **Unlimited Support**: maxPerNamespace = 0 means unlimited policies\n3. **Event Handling**:\n   - Upsert: Increments count (handles both new and updated policies)\n   - Delete: Decrements count (safe even if count is 0)\n   - Sync: Acknowledges API server sync completion\n4. **Resource Pattern**: Integrates with Cilium's resource watching framework\n5. **Logging**: Uses structured logging for debugging and monitoring\n\n## Testing Strategy\n\nThe test suite provides comprehensive coverage:\n- Unit tests for individual
